Microsoft Windows[R] NT Version 3.51
Hardware Compatibility List

=========================================================================
The following computers and peripherals have been tested and are supported
with the released version of Windows NT 3.51.  Some computers may be sold with
peripherals that are not yet supported by the Windows NT operating system,
or that require a device driver supplied by the manufacturer. We have not
tested every computer and/or device in all possible configurations.
Please refer to the Release Notes for additional compatibility information
when installing Windows NT 3.51.

Included as an addendum is the Windows NT 3.51 PowerPC Hardware Compatibility 
Section.  Refer to this section for information regarding tested PowerPC 
architecture systems and devices.

If you encounter problems while running Windows NT 3.51,
please file a bug report by filling out 'PROBREP.TXT' located in the \i386
directory on Windows NT 3.51 CD-ROM or floppy disk #2 of the Windows NT 3.51
installation disks and submit it as instructed in PROBREP.TXT.

Items listed with footnote number [1] require one of the device drivers
available in the \DRVLIB directory on the Windows NT 3.51 CD-ROM.

Updates to these lists will appear in Library 1 of the WINNT (GO WINNT)
forum or Library 17 of the MSWIN32 forum (GO MSWIN32) on CompuServe[R]
Information Services.
=========================================================================

Color Depths                  Display modes in the "other" column
---------------------------    -----------------------------------
16 = 16 colors                     A 640x400x256
256 = 256 colors                   B 1040x768x256
32k = 32,768 colors                C 1104x828x256
65k = 65,536 colors                D 1152x864x256
16.7m = 16.7 million colors        E 1152x864x65k
        (24 bits per pixel)        F 1152x864xTRUE
TRUE = True Color                  G 1182x882x256
       (16.7m accelerated)         H 1182x882x65k
                                   I 1182x882x16.7m
                                   J 1600x1200x256
                                   K 1600x1200x65k
                                   L 1024x864x256
                                   M 1024x864xTRUE
                                   N 1152x864x16.7m
                                   O 1152x864x16
                                   P 1152x900x256
                                   Q 1152x900xTRUE

Display adapters not listed above are expected to work on x86 systems if they
use the following supported chip sets. Install first as Standard VGA, then
select the corresponding driver from the Display Applet in the Control Panel.

Manufacturer     Chip Set             Driver    Color Depths               Max Res.       
------------     --------             ------    ------------               --------       
IBM              8514/a               8514A     256                        1024x768       
                 XGA                  XGA       256                        1040x768       
                 XGA-2                XGA       256                        1104x828

Windows NT 3.51 PowerPC[TM] Hardware Compatibility Section
======================================================
The following systems, based on the PowerPC processor, and peripherals have
been tested and are considered compatible with the Windows NT 3.51 product.


PowerPC Supported Hardware
=========================================================================
Refer to the main body of this Hardware Compatibility List for compatibility
information for the following hardware catagories.  All entries in these
catagories are supported on the PowerPC platform except as noted.

SCSI CD-ROM Drives
SCSI Tape Drives
SCSI Removable Media
SCSI Hard Drives
Storage Cabinets
RAID Systems
Video Capture Adapters
Uninterruptible Power Supplies
Hardware Security Hosts
ISDN Adapters
Third Party Remote Access Servers
Modems
Printers

=========================================================================

  System

SCSI Host Adapters
=========================================================================
The following SCSI adapters have been tested on the PowerPC platform
with the following CD-ROM, tape, fixed and removable drives (except as noted):
ArchiveST 4000 DAT, CD-Technologies CD Porta-Drive T-3401, NEC Intersect
CDR-74, Micropolis 1924, Peripheral Land Infinity 88, Procom Technology MCD-DS,
Syquest 5110, Toshiba TXM-3401E, WangTek 5150es.

   BUS   SCSI Host Adapter                        
-------- ---------------------------------------- 
 ISA-16  Adaptec AHA-1522                         
 ISA-16  Adaptec AHA-1522A                        
   PCI   Adaptec AHA-2940                         
 ISA-16  COMPAQ 6260 SCSI-2 Controller

the same resolutions and scan frequencies as your display adapter.  Please
refer to README.WRI for more information on display support.  All Video adapters
listed below require that the host computer provide support in the firmware for
third party add-in video(INT 10), unless otherwise noted.

Technical Notes
=========================================================================
The Windows NT Driver Library is provided on the Windows NT CD-ROM in the
\DRVLIB directory, as well as several locations for electronic transmission.
Please see the section at the end of this document for instructions on
downloading and accessing Windows NT Driver Library drivers.

     1  This device requires a driver from the \DRVLIB directory on the
        Windows NT CD-ROM, or the Windows NT Driver Library.
     2  This device requires a driver from the Windows NT driver Library. 
        See the following section on accessing these drivers.
     3  System requires ALR EISA Config utility 2.13 or later to enable
        COM ports in Windows NT.
     4  External Cache must be disabled to run Windows NT.
     5  Requires AST BIOS Rev. 1.02 to install and run Windows NT.
     6  Requires AST BIOS Rev. 2.03 to install and run Windows NT.
     7  Must copy ABIOS.SYS and *.BIO from reference diskette to root
        directory of boot drive to install Windows NT on this system.
     8  Requires the IBM RAID Controller v2.0 driver located in Windows NT
        Driver Library.
     9  This system only supports 640x480x16 video resolution.
    10  Refer to SETUP.TXT on the Windows NT 3.51 CDROM for information on
        configuring this machine/device before installation.
    11  Contact Panasonic at 1-800-LAPTOP5 for CD-ROM compatibility with
        Windows NT 3.51.
    12  To install Windows NT on this system SCSI detection must be
        skipped during setup.
    13  Refer to setup.txt to properly configure this system for printing
        in Windows NT.
    14  Contact the manufacturer for information on running Windows NT on
        this machine.
    15  Requires AMD Bios Revision 0.02.18 to function as a multiprocessor
        system.
    16  This system requires Windows Sound System driver to enable sound.
    17  Floppy drive not supported on this system when running off of
        Battery power.
    18  If the Port Replicator is used with this model, PCMCIA netcards
        are not supported configured at IRQ 10 or 11 and I/O Port 300.
    19  PCMCIA devices cannot be present in this model during Windows NT
        3.51 setup.
    20  PCMCIA netcards not supported at I/O port 300 on this model.
    21  PCMCIA netcards are not supported when using IRQ 10 on this model.
    22  PCMCIA hard drives not supported on this model.
    23  PCMCIA network adapters not supported when configured at IRQ 10 on
        this model.
    24  This adapter has been verified to work with Network Monitor
    25  Supported on x86 only.
    26  For best performance, this adapter should be configured to IRQ-11.
    27  Tape drives are not supported with this adapter.
    28  Tested with firmware revisions 3.10 and 3.20.
    29  This adapter requires an active terminator for proper performance.
    30  The floppy controller on this adapter is not supported.
    31  This adapter must be configured for 5 MB/second asynchronous I/O
        to work with listed CD-ROM drives from NEC.
    32  This adapter must be configured for 5 MB/second asynchronous I/O
        to work with listed CD-ROM drives from Chinon, Hitachi, and NEC.
    33  Tested with the Unisys PW2 Advantage 3256 (Flemington).
    34  AIC-7770c and AIC-7770e are supported.
    35  Tested with the Unisys PW2 Advantage Plus MPE 4668.
    36  Removable media drives are not supported with cache enabled.
    37  Tested with Compaq Deskpro XL 466 and HP Vectra XU 5/90c.
    38  Scanners are not supported with this adapter.
    39  Tested with Firmware rev. 6D4(3B0).
    40  To use this adapter, at least one device on the bus must provide
        termination power.
    41  Refer to SETUP.TXT for information on configuring this adapter.
    42  Removable media is not supported with this adapter.
    43  This adapter does not support the WangTek 5150es tape drive.
    44  SCSI BIOS dated before 1991 requires PS/2 Reference Diskette
        version 1.12 or later.
    45  This adapter cannot be used for CD Setup.  To install Windows NT
        with this adapter, use the WINNT.EXE Setup method.
    46  The driver for this adapter defaults to IRQ-15.
    47  Tested with NEC RISCstation 2000.

        (Digital Equipment Corp. 2100 Server model A500MP).

    52  This driver is not supported on Multi-Processor computers.
    53  This adapter is only supported on IRQ-5.

        TMC-850M and TMC-1670 adapters.

        AHA-1742 adapters.

        NT.

        with Windows NT.

        models only.

        with Windows NT.
    66  This drive is not supported with the Adaptec AHA-1640 adapter.

How To Find New Drivers in the Windows NT Driver Library (WNTDL)
================================================================

COMPUSERVE
----------
A.  If you are using WinCIM[SM]:
	1.  From the Services menu, select GO.
	2.  Type MSL in the GO dialog box.
	3.  Select 2 to scan.
	4.  Search for WNTDL to view the whole WNTDL list or another 
            key word to view specific files.
B.  If you are not using WinCIM, log onto CompuServe, type GO
    MSL, then follow instructions 3 and 4 above.

ONLINE
------
A.  Log onto OnLine.
	1.  From the Database menu, select the option to Select DB.
	2.  Choose the Software Library option.
	3.  From the Software Library option, select the option Host
            Items.
	4.  In the Query box, type WNTDL to review the whole WNTDL
            list or another key word to view a specific file.
B.  To get more information on a specific file, highlight the file with
    the cursor and press <Enter>. This brings up more details
    about the file.

GENie[TM]
---------
Log onto Genie.
	1.  From the main menu, select option 5 - Computing Services.
	2.  From the Computing Services menu, select option 6 - 
            IBM PC/TANDY Roundtables.
	3.  From the IBM PC/TANDY Roundtables menu, select option 3 - 
            Software Libraries.
	4.  From the Software Libraries Menu, select option 3 - Search 
            File Directory.
	5.  Type WNTDL as the search string to view the WNTDL list or 
            any other key word to view a specific file.

MICROSOFT DOWN LOAD SERVICES
----------------------------
Log onto MSDL by calling (206) 936-6735.
	1.  Enter name and location.
	2.  From the main menu, press F for File index.
	3.  Select L to list the whole WNTDL list or E to examine a 
           specific file.

IF YOU DO NOT HAVE A MODEM
--------------------------
You can obtain an individual driver from the WNTDL on a disk by
calling Microsoft Product Support Services at (206) 637-7098.

While we have endeavored to supply as complete and accurate a list as
possible, MICROSOFT MAKES NO WARRANTIES, EXPRESS OR IMPLIED, AS TO THE
COMPLETENESS AND ACCURACY OF THIS LIST.  This list does not constitute an
endorsement of any particular manufacturer.

Microsoft and BallPoint are registered trademarks and Windows and
Windows NT are trademarks of Microsoft Corporation.
